The \r\n<a href="../ads.html">UIUC Airfoil Data Site</a> gives some background\r\non the database.  The airfoils are listed alphabetically by the airfoil filename (which is usually close to the airfoil name).\r\nAnswers to frequently asked questions are posted\r\nhere <a href="../ads_faq.html">Airfoils FAQ</a> and for the most\r\nrecent changes see the\r\n<a href="../ads_history.html">update history</a>.</p>\r\n\r\n<hr />\r\n\r\n<b>\r\n&nbsp;\r\n<a href="#Z">Z</a>&nbsp;.&nbsp;\r\n<a href="#TOP">top</a></b><br>\r\n\r\n<hr /> \r\n\r\n<h3><span>Other Useful Sources / Mirrors</span><img src="../headers/h3_coord_database_otherSources.png" width="845" height="26" alt="Other Useful Sources / Mirrors" /></h3>\r\n\r\n<ul>\r\n\r\n<li> <a href="../ads/aircraft.html">The Incomplete Guide to Airfoil Usage</a>: A useful aircraft/airfoil "reverse lookup" database from David Lednicer </li>\r\n\r\n<li>In addition to the links below, more airfoil-info links can be found back at the <a href="../ads.html">UIUC Airfoil Data Site homepage</a></li>\r\n\r\n<!--\r\n<li>NASG site includes useful search features and\r\npolars: <a href="http://www.nasg.com/afdb/index-e.phtml">http://www.nasg.com/afdb/index-e.phtml</a></li>\r\n-->\r\n\r\n<li>Includes DXF and IGS files: <a href="http://isoar.ca/~andrewm/rc/airfoils/">http://isoar.ca/~andrewm/rc/airfoils/</a>, <a href="http://isoar.ca/~andrewm/">http://isoar.ca/~andrewm/</a></li>\r\n\r\n<li>Python scripts for converting .dat text files to SVG format files: <a href="https://github.com/jdcasey/airfoil-utils">https://github.com/jdcasey/airfoil-utils</a></li>\r\n\r\n<li>Searchable web engine that includes the UIUC Airfoil Coordinates Database:\r\n<a href="http://www.worldofkrauss.com/">Airfoil Investigation Database</a>\r\n\r\n\r\n<li>TraCFoil airfoil and rib plotting program for models: \r\n    <a href="http://tracfoil.free.fr/tracfoil/accueilE.htm">http://tracfoil.free.fr/tracfoil/accueilE.htm</a></li>\r\n\r\n<li>Martin Hepperle\'s site, including airfoil coordinates (mostly listed here as well) and lots\r\nof other information: <a href="http://www.mh-aerotools.de/airfoils/">http://www.mh-aerotools.de/airfoils/</a></li>\r\n\r\n<li>Model airplane site, mostly focused on flying wings: <br />\r\n<a href="http://www.aerodesign.de/">http://www.aerodesign.de/</a>\r\nand <a href="http://www.aerodesign.de/profile/profile_m.htm">http://www.aerodesign.de/profile/profile_m.htm</a></li>\r\n\r\n<li>Helmut Quabeck website and airfoils:\r\n<a href="http://www.hq-modellflug.de/">http://www.hq-modellflug.de/</a></li>\r\n\r\n<li>NACA Report 93 (1921) includes coordinates and wind tunnel data on\r\nseveral vintage airfoils, e.g. the 1903 Wright Flyer airfoil called\r\nthe "Eiffel 10" in the report.</li>\r\n\r\n<li><a href="http://www.texample.net/tikz/examples/airfoil-profiles/">Airfoils in TeX</a>: Want to include your airfoils in LaTeX/TeX format? This site describes how.</li>\r\n\r\n<li>GestProf commercial airfoil viewer program: <a href="http://a190754.free.fr/PROFILS.HTM">http://a190754.free.fr/PROFILS.HTM</a></li>\r\n\r\n\r\n</ul>\r\n\r\n<hr />\r\n<b>\r\n&nbsp;\r\n<a href="#A">A</a>&nbsp;.&nbsp;\r\n<a
